read_int_from_ini_file 7@ = get_int_from_ini_file "cleo\Debugmenu.ini" section "Values" key "Skin_ID_To_Change"
wait 0
    not 7@ <= -1
    jf @SNIPPET_01
        not 7@ >= 353
        jf @SNIPPET_01
        wait 250
            if and
            7@ >= 290
            7@ <= 351
            then gosub @SNIPPET_17
            else if 7@ == 352
                then gosub @DEBUG6_41
                else
                Model.Load(7@)
                038B: load_requested_models
                09C7: change_player $PLAYER_CHAR model_to 7@
                Model.Destroy(7@)
                write_memory CLOTHES_DAT_AND_PLAYER_IMG_PATCH size 5 value 0x90 virtual_protect 0
                    7@ == 0
                    jf @SNIPPET_01
                    write_memory 0x5A834D size 1 value 0xE8 virtual_protect 0
                    write_memory 0x5A834E size 1 value 0x8E virtual_protect 0
                    write_memory 0x5A834F size 1 value 0xFE virtual_protect 0
                    write_memory 0x5A8350 size 1 value 0xFF virtual_protect 0
                    write_memory 0x5A8351 size 1 value 0xFF virtual_protect 0
                end
            end
cleo_return 0

:DEBUG1_A1    
wait 0
    if is_key_pressed 38
    then 7@ += 1
    else if is_key_pressed 40
        then 7@ -= 1
        else if is_key_pressed 39
            then 16@ += 1
            076D: get_zone 1@s gang 16@ density_to 7@
            else if is_key_pressed 37
                then 16@ -= 1
                076D: get_zone 1@s gang 16@ density_to 7@
                else if is_key_pressed 32
                    then 
                    076C: set_zone 1@s gang 16@ density_to 7@
                    0879: enable_gang_wars true 
                    08AC: hide_gang_zones_on_map false 
                    090D: highlight_all_inactive_gang_zones_as_available_for_gangwars
                    else
                    gosub @SNIPPET_04
                        if or
                        is_key_pressed 5@
                        is_key_pressed 6@
                        jf @DEBUG2_A1
                        cleo_return 0
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
jump @DEBUG2_A1

:DEBUG2_A1
wait 0
    if 16@ == 0
    then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG9U' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
    else if 16@ == 1
        then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG9S' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
        else if 16@ == 2
            then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG9T' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
            else if 16@ == 3
                then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG6A' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
                else if 16@ == 4
                    then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG6C' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
                    else if 16@ == 5
                        then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG6D' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
                        else if 16@ == 6
                            then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG6E' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
                            else if 16@ == 7
                                then 01E5: show_text_1number_highpriority GXT 'DEBUG6F' number 7@ time 100 flag 1
                                else
                                16@ = 0
                                076D: get_zone 1@s gang 16@ density_to 7@
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
jump @DEBUG1_A1

:Get_Date_Time 
allocate_memory 1@ size 30
allocate_memory 4@ size 256
allocate_memory 5@ size 256
string_format 4@ = format "nodatefound"
string_format 5@ = format "nodatefound"
0AA2: 2@ = load_library "kernel32.dll" //IF and SET
    if 0AA4: 3@ = get_proc_address "GetLocalTime" library 2@
    then
    write_memory 1@ size 2 value 1 virtual_protect 1
    call_function 3@ num_params 1 pop 0 1@
    0085: 31@ = 1@ // (int)
    read_memory result 20@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1
    31@ += 2
    read_memory result 21@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1
    31@ += 4                  
    read_memory result 23@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1                    
    31@ += 2
    read_memory result 24@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1
    31@ += 2
    read_memory result 25@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1
    31@ += 2
    read_memory result 26@ memory 31@ size 2 virtual_protect 1
    string_format 4@ = format "~y~Date=%d.%d.%d" 23@ 21@ 20@
    string_format 5@ = format "~y~Time=%d:%d:%d" 24@ 25@ 26@
    end
0AA3: free_library 2@
free_memory 1@
cleo_return 2 4@ 5@
